# Welcome | Football Widgets | API 3.0

The easiest way to show all important football data is by copying and pasting a short line of code into your web application. Easy-to-use football widgets are available for everyone!

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/football-widgets#optimise-your-workflow-and-save-resources)

OPTIMISE YOUR WORKFLOW AND SAVE RESOURCES

With Sportmonks Football Widgets, you will save time and resources.

*   The Football Widgets are easy to implement and even easier to use. Because from the moment you implement the football widgets, you don´t have to do anything anymore.
    
*   Maintenance is done by our developers, and the widgets will request our API every time it is needed.
    
*   Our Football widgets were created by developers who are passionate about football and dedicated to providing you with the best experience possible.
    

We constantly seek to improve and expand our documentation. If you think something is missing, have an idea for a great tutorial or how-to guide, or have any other questions, don't hesitate to contact us! We value your input. Contact us at [\[email protected\]](https://docs.sportmonks.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection)
.

name

latitude

longitude

Query Parameters

Required?

Description

`api_token`

YES

Your unique API token

`include`

NO

Enrich the API with more data by using includes

`select`

NO

Select specific fields on the base entity

`filters`

NO

Filter the API response on multiple related entities. There are static filters and dynamic filters.

Please find the possibilities in the Static and Dynamic Filter tab.

Not applicable for this endpoint.

The **dynamic filters** are based on entities and includes. Each dynamic filter uses an entity to filter on and one entity to apply the filter on. Below are examples with explanations of how filters are set up. For more information, please look at our Filters page.

Dynamic Filters

Available on Entity

Description

Examples

`regions`

Coaches, Leagues, Players, Teams, and way more. Check this [endpointarrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/football2/v/core/endpoints/filters/get-all-entity-filters)
 for all possibilities.

Filter regions and more based on cities.

`&include=regions&filters=regionCities:regionIDS`

No

You can use a total of `4` nested includes on this endpoint

Include options

[`region`](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/core-api/entities/core#region)

**Related Entities:**

*   [City](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/core-api/entities/core#city)

GET All Countries\
\
Filter all countries starting from a certain country ID. Handy if you're doing an import for all countries and want to continue from a certain ID.\
\
`&filters=IdAfter:countryID`\
\
The **dynamic filters** are based on entities and includes. Each dynamic filter uses an entity to filter on and one entity to apply the filter on. Below are examples with explanations of how filters are set up. For more information, please look at our Filters page.\
\
Dynamic Filters\
\
Available on Entity\
\
Description\
\
Examples\
\
`regions`\
\
Region Check this [endpointarrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/football2/v/core/endpoints/filters/get-all-entity-filters)\
 for all possibilities.\
\
Filter regions based on countries.\
\
`&include=regions&filters=regionCountries:regionIDS`\
\
`leagues`\
\
Check this [endpointarrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/football2/v/core/endpoints/filters/get-all-entity-filters)\
 for all possibilities.\
\
Filter leagues based on countries.\
\
`&include=leagues&filters=leagueCountries:leagueIDS`\
\
#### \
\

    require "uri"\
    require "net/http"\
    \
    url = URI("https://api.sportmonks.com/v3/core/countries?api_token={your_token}")\
    \
    https = Net::HTTP.new(url.host, url.port)\
    https.use_ssl = true\
    \
    request = Net::HTTP::Get.new(url)\
    \
    response = https.request(request)\
    puts response.read_body\
    \

Copy\

    import http.client\
    \
    conn = http.client.HTTPSConnection("api.sportmonks.com")\
    payload = ''\
    headers = {}\
    conn.request("GET", "/v3/core/countries?api_token={your_token}", payload, headers)\
    res = conn.getresponse()\
    data = res.read()\
    print(data.decode("utf-8"))\

      .build();\

      .url("https://api.sportmonks.com/v3/core/countries?api_token={your_token}")\
      .method("GET", null)\
      .build();\
    Response response = client.newCall(request).execute();\

Copy\
\
    var unirest = require('unirest');\
    var req = unirest('GET', 'https://api.sportmonks.com/v3/core/countries?api_token={your_token}')\
      .end(function (res) { \
        if (res.error) throw new Error(res.error); \
        console.log(res.raw_body);\
      });\
\
Copy\
\
    package main\
    \
    import (\
      "fmt"\
      "net/http"\
      "io/ioutil"\
    )\
    \
    func main() {\
    \
      url := "https://api.sportmonks.com/v3/core/countries?api_token={your_token}"\
      method := "GET"\
    \
      client := &http.Client {\
      }\
      req, err := http.NewRequest(method, url, nil)\
    \
      if err != nil {\
        fmt.Println(err)\
        return\
      }\
      res, err := client.Do(req)\
      if err != nil {\
        fmt.Println(err)\
        return\
      }\
      defer res.Body.Close()\
    \
      body, err := ioutil.ReadAll(res.Body)\
      if err != nil {\
        fmt.Println(err)\
        return\
      }\
      fmt.Println(string(body))\
    }\

# Configurations | Football Widgets | API 3.0

The configuration options are essential to fit the widgets into your application or website. In the Match Centre widget, you can select the country, league, season, stage and fixture.

In the livescore widget, you can select a customised list of (max 25) leagues you want to showcase or show all leagues in your widget subscription.

You can show or hide the following:

1.  Header
    
2.  Team logos
    
3.  Player images
    
4.  Match Center (advanced)
    
5.  Theme switch (light or dark mode)
    

You can change the font, title and, last but not least, the primary, sub-primary, secondary and tertiary colours.

For more information about the configuration options you can check out our [configuration page.](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/football-widgets/our-widgets/configurations)

![](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3244704705-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWspgZhERqy7nYPTldGhL%252Fuploads%252FCjdAknthjzIX3ayDUAu1%252FBasic%2520vs%2520Advanced%2520%28Livescore%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D58fff7bc-b767-45a6-b1a8-8d61e0de62f2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a2fb3034&sv=2)

# Livescores | Football Widgets | API 3.0

The Livescores Widget is a widget which shows a complete schedule of the day. All leagues included in your widget subscription are provided for that particular day. You can switch to any day in the past or future as well.

By clicking on the game's score, you can see information about the events of any particular match.

Last but not least, the advanced version of this widget allows you to include the Match Centre within this widget as well. Let's dive into what the Livescore widget can do.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/football-widgets/our-widgets/livescore-widgets/livescores#functionalities)

Functionalities

When people visit your widget, the first thing they will see is an overview of all fixtures that are played that day. The fixtures shown depend on your widget subscription and the configuration of your widget.

Per fixture, a match tile is displayed with both team names and live scores. Also, the game's status is shown (e.g. FT, NS) or if a fixture is LIVE, the current minute of the game. The most important events of a match (cards and goals) can be viewed by clicking on a match tile.

If you have the widget's advanced variant, you can show a ‘details’ link leading to the [Match Centre](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/football-widgets/our-widgets/livescore-widgets/match-centre)
.

![](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3244704705-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWspgZhERqy7nYPTldGhL%252Fuploads%252FgEI0LqnRsvD6U4IQkPAq%252Fmatch_tile_livescore_widget.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2706e121-cbe1-4cb3-8301-8890566698f4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6ef2f605&sv=2)

Livescore Widget overview

Besides viewing the list of today's matches, the livescore overview page also has a couple of handy functionalities. You can filter on a specific league with the league select function and search on teams with the search bar. You can also view only inplay fixtures by clicking the LIVE button. And lastly, you can view schedules/results of other days using the calendar or the date buttons.

![](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3244704705-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWspgZhERqy7nYPTldGhL%252Fuploads%252FtNJDhlfptG71XbZzkf7N%252Fdate_option_livescore_widget.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2d01f88a-945e-4cfc-9574-f9daed506787&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c6d64849&sv=2)

Use the calender

# Schedule | Football Widgets | API 3.0

The Schedule Widget shows the complete schedule of the league you have selected. You will see the status of the game, the time it starts, or the score once the game is live. Furthermore, you can see dates and all match events.

![](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3244704705-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWspgZhERqy7nYPTldGhL%252Fuploads%252FN0l6aMLIjUfQZwfhXpVQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D84159b94-af5d-4a61-bb15-1df8ffcd0d36&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=62ee8ec3&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/football-widgets/our-widgets/league-widgets/schedule#basic-versus-advanced)

Basic versus advanced

The advanced Schedule Widget offers the option to showcase a complete Match Centre. This provides a lot of extra information about the scheduled and finished matches. For example, when a game is finished, it offers all kinds of stats, lineup details and more. When the game is Not Started, you can find H2H results, total results and form of both parties. You can find everything the Match Centre widget offers in the [Match Centre section.](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/football-widgets/our-widgets/livescore-widgets/match-centre)

# Standings | Football Widgets | API 3.0

The Standings Widget shows the complete table of the league you have selected. And by complete, we mean everything you expect to see in any league table is available.

You will see the position a team is in and what this ranking means at the end of the season. For example, will a team in the number 3 spot play in play-offs for a particular tournament (for example, the Champions League), and will the number 20 be relegated? These standing rules can be found by watching for the colour in front of the ranking a particular team is in and checking this colour at the bottom of the league. Besides that, the logo of the team and the team name are included in the standings table.

Next to the basic information about the teams, we will find the number of games a specific team has played (P) and the matches that a team has won (W), drawn (D) or lost (L). After that, goals for (GF), goals against (GA), goal difference (GD) and points (Pts) are shown. You can even decide to show the form of every team behind the points. This way, you can show their last five matches' results (win, draw, lose).

![](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3244704705-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWspgZhERqy7nYPTldGhL%252Fuploads%252FAe2hUfSibpAtbKgjgqpT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da6b7361f-71bc-47d0-b77e-6aee91871021&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=616938fc&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/football-widgets/our-widgets/league-widgets/standings#basic-versus-advanced)

Basic versus advanced

The extras you will receive when using the advanced version of the Standings widgets are as followed:

1.  Live standings
    
2.  Season filter
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/football-widgets/our-widgets/league-widgets/standings#live-standings)

Live standings

You can include live standings using the advanced standings widget. But what does that mean? When a fixture is live, there is a score for that particular game. For example, Arsenal has 41 points before the match starts. At the start of the match, the score is 0-0. Because of the live standings, Arsenal will now be on 42 points. When Arsenal is in the lead (let's say 1-0), the team will have 41+3 points in the live standings. In short, the virtual result of a live match will be included in the standings if you decide to use live standings.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/football-widgets/our-widgets/league-widgets/standings#season-filter)

Season filter:

You will have access to all seasons Sportmonks provides of the leagues you have included in your widget subscription. This means you can select any season you want to use the standings. Are you interested in that season your favourite team won the league? Show your pride and put it on your website by selecting the specific season. More interested in finding out which team became champion in a particular season? Easily select that season to find out about the standings.

![](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3244704705-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWspgZhERqy7nYPTldGhL%252Fuploads%252FehlhRsdfqlCGEKb4EkdP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D45356d32-a634-4cb5-af16-2ce7f38d6b3d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d57b78a7&sv=2)

Last updated 2 years ago

Was this helpful?

Was this helpful?

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Configurations | Football Widgets | API 3.0

The configuration options are essential to fit the schedule widget into your application or website. You select the country and league you want to showcase. After that, you can choose if you will show the schedule of a specific round or not. When ‘by round’ is on, the schedule is shown per the current round or stage of a season. When turned off, the latest seven and upcoming three fixtures are shown by default. You can show or hide the following:

1.  Header
    
2.  Team logos
    
3.  League logos
    
4.  Match Center (advanced)
    
5.  Theme switch (light or dark mode)
    

You can change the font, and last but not least, you can change the Primary, sub-primary, secondary and tertiary colours.

There are multiple configuration options, but the most important options are to choose the country and league. After that, you can select the group of statistics you want to showcase. You don’t have to choose, though.

However, you can filter on a group of statistics. For example, if you only want to show everything about goals, you can select this group, and your users can see only the goals scored and those conceded statistics.

![](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3244704705-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWspgZhERqy7nYPTldGhL%252Fuploads%252FV9kXDhSN4xU7ELIau3OM%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0d8fd08f-2ea7-422b-a6d7-3476e82d0887&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4dd36ca6&sv=2)

Another thing you can do with these filters is to create a filter of all statistics you want to showcase. For example, you want to combine cards and tackles, goals and possession %, or goals and cards.

![](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3244704705-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWspgZhERqy7nYPTldGhL%252Fuploads%252FBcWVLfM5bMK6eL3jnBo8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df4b1ecf5-b9fd-46fe-9d3a-189f3b1ac77e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=35eb3b7a&sv=2)

You can show a season filter if you have the advanced version of the Widget. Show or hide the header and team logos. We also suggest changing the title to customise it in your app and website.

circle-info

Keep in mind this title will only be visible with a certain width. If the Widget is too small, the title will disappear.

Besides, there are options to set the Widget to light- or dark mode and show or hide the theme switch. Finally, you can change the primary, sub-primary, secondary, and tertiary colours.

For more information about the configuration options you can check out our [configuration page.](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/football-widgets/our-widgets/configurations)

![](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3244704705-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWspgZhERqy7nYPTldGhL%252Fuploads%252FUPj1CDwYqKn5hum4JntP%252FBasic%2520vs%2520Advanced%2520%28League%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8b8fa820-6d75-4813-bf1e-f3caf5566b06&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=787d7012&sv=2)

# Team statistics | Football Widgets | API 3.0

The Team Statistics Widget shows all teams and their statistics in the league. All teams will be ranked based on the statistic you have selected. When you choose the statistic goals, you will see how all the teams rank based on the goals they scored. Do you want to see which team has the most possession on average? Select the Ball Possession % statistic and determine which teams have much possession and which don’t. All statistics available are:

1.  Goals
    
2.  Ball Possession %
    
3.  Corners
    
4.  Attacks
    
5.  Dangerous Attacks
    
6.  Offsides
    
7.  Fouls
    
8.  Tackles
    
9.  Yellow Cards
    
10.  Red Cards
    
11.  Yellowred Cards
    
12.  Goals Conceded
    
13.  Clean sheets
    
14.  Team Wins
    
15.  Team Draws
    
16.  Team Lost
    

![](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3244704705-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWspgZhERqy7nYPTldGhL%252Fuploads%252FWoNak8JQu9PIFHNBgENw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3441ac6c-4bd4-45fa-a8c3-852306cddeef&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2efd6dcb&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/football-widgets/our-widgets/league-widgets/team-statistics#basic-versus-advanced)

Basic versus advanced

In the advanced version of the Widget, you can show a season filter. This filter lets you and your users select the season you want to see. Show the statistics of teams all the way back to 2005.

circle-info

Please note that we have the most detailed statistics from the 2017 season. Before that season, there were mostly basic stats available.

# Topscorers | Football Widgets | API 3.0

The Topscorers Widget shows the topscorers all the way back to 2005 per season. You will see the player, the team, the nationality and the amount of goals. Also, the most assist, yellow cards and red cards top scorers are included in this Widget.

![](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3244704705-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWspgZhERqy7nYPTldGhL%252Fuploads%252F3n7a2HEFQSmSp2foqh2L%252FTop%2520scorers%2520La%2520liga.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3daaa7de-6a54-4402-87e3-2d13c585a9ce&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b2335cb1&sv=2)

**Basic versus advanced**

When using the advanced option, you will receive the following additions:

1.  Colours customisation
    
2.  Custom brand
    

Colours customisation

You can adapt the complete table of top scorers into your own corporate identity. Designing tables ensures a professional and consistent look and differentiates your company from your competitors.

Custom brand

Looking at the bottom of the basic Topscorer Widget, you can see the Sportmonks logo. With the advanced option you can change the this to your own brand logo.

![](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3244704705-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWspgZhERqy7nYPTldGhL%252Fuploads%252F1l08wtg89Oxijte1PaJI%252FDifference%2520basic%2520advanced.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D13e66275-122a-4733-9f7e-6311f5987bb0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=60b87c84&sv=2)

**Also, is it possible to configure a couple of things on your hand**

*   Choose your competition/team
    
*   Custom the number of rows
    
*   Make the team/league logo visible or not
    
*   Highlight one individual team
    
*   Decide on whether to have our header or not
    
*   Dark mode
    
*   Customise colours
    

circle-info

Please note that we have the most detailed statistics from the 2005 season. Before that season, there were mostly basic stats available.

Last updated 2 years ago

# Squads | Football Widgets | API 3.0

The Squad Widgets shows all players of the team you are interested in. You can choose to show all players that have been part of the squad during the whole season or only to show the players currently in the team. Think about players that have made a transfer or went out on loan.

![](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3244704705-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWspgZhERqy7nYPTldGhL%252Fuploads%252F21SzyX9WEywYyg4LTcF3%252Fsquad_psg.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dea529102-9814-4970-89d4-ab5cd4346229&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=13a3d013&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/football-widgets/our-widgets/team-widgets/squads#player-information)

Player information

So, what will you find in the squad widget besides the players? Well, you can find all kinds of player information. First up, we have the jersey number every player wears. After that, we have an image of the face of the players, the name, positions and ages of the players. You can sort on the players' number, position, name and age. Furthermore, you will be able to see all nationalities in the squad. Each player is shown with their nationality.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/football-widgets/our-widgets/team-widgets/squads#player-statistics)

Player statistics

After the player information, all kinds of player statistics are shown. The stats are as follows:

1.  Games played
    
2.  Starting 11
    
3.  Subbed in
    
4.  Subbed out
    
5.  Goals scored
    
6.  Assists
    
7.  Yellow cards
    
8.  Red cards
    
9.  Yellowred cards
    
10.  Minutes played
    
11.  Rating
    

You can order all players based on all of their stats. For example, if you want to see who is the highest or lowest-rated player, you can click on the arrows to show a descending or ascending order of the ratings of players. The same goes for any of the other statistics.

You can choose any country, any league and any team that is included in your widget subscription.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/football-widgets/our-widgets/team-widgets/squads#basic-versus-advanced)

Basic versus advanced

Make your users relive older seasons by making use of the advanced version. This enables you to make use of a season filter. More information about this can be found on our [configurations page.](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/football-widgets/our-widgets/team-widgets/configurations)

For example, the 2010 squad of Barcelona:

![](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3244704705-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWspgZhERqy7nYPTldGhL%252Fuploads%252FBXxjD0CCfSQq2BXI8Fmy%252Fimage%2520%282%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9fc46277-9c92-4173-8d77-49f63b19a28f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bfbcf57a&sv=2)

Last updated 2 years ago

Was this helpful?

# Configurations | Football Widgets | API 3.0

The configuration options are essential to fit the widgets into your application or website.

You select the country, league and team you want to showcase. You can show or hide the following:

1.  Header
    
2.  Team logos
    
3.  Player images
    
4.  Match Center (advanced)
    
5.  Theme switch (light or dark mode)
    
6.  Season filter
    

You can change the font, title and last but not least, you can change the Primary, sub-primary, secondary and tertiary colours.

For more information about the configuration options, you can check out our [configuration page.](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/football-widgets/our-widgets/configurations)

![](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3244704705-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWspgZhERqy7nYPTldGhL%252Fuploads%252FGktfdr9wcoXQA36WlQRU%252FBasic%2520vs%2520Advanced%2520%28Team%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D13dfe4c7-429e-447e-95ac-e9b0fb256429&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bc11904b&sv=2)

# GET My Usage | Core API 3.0 | API 3.0

circle-info

We retain user request logs for approximately two months, after which they are automatically deleted.

Base URL

Example Response

Field Description

Copy

    https://api.sportmonks.com/v3/my/usage

Copy

    {
        id: 98564461,
        endpoint: "api.sports.livescores.inplay",
        count: 1374,
        entity: "fixture",
        remaining_requests: 50878,
        period_start: 1694682000,
        period_end: 1694682300
    },
    {
        id: 98160610,
        endpoint: "api.sports.fixtures.show",
        count: 748,
        entity: "fixture",
        remaining_requests: 52252,
        period_start: 1694635200,
        period_end: 1694635500
    },

Field

Description

id

identifier of the record

endpoint

identifier of the requested endpoint

count

total calls for the given timeframe

entity

the entity the rate limit applies on

remaining\_requests

amount of requests remaining for the entity in the hourly rate limit

period\_start

timestamp representing the aggregation start time

period\_end

timestamp representing the aggregation end time

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/core-api/my-sportmonks/get-my-usage#parameters)

Parameters

Query Parameters

Required?

Description

`api_token`

YES

Your unique API token

`include`

NO

Enrich the API with more data by using includes

`select`

NO

Select specific fields on the base entity

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/core-api/my-sportmonks/get-my-usage#pagination)

Pagination

YES

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/core-api/my-sportmonks/get-my-usage#include-depth)

Include depth

Using includes is not supported on this endpoint.

# GET My Enrichments | Core API 3.0 | API 3.0

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/core-api/my-sportmonks/get-my-enrichments#parameters)

Parameters

Query Parameters

Required?

Description

`api_token`

YES

Your unique API token

`include`

NO

Enrich the API with more data by using includes

`select`

NO

Select specific fields on the base entity

`other parameters`

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    require "uri"
    require "net/http"
    
    url = URI("https://api.sportmonks.com/v3/my/enrichments?api_token={your_token}")
    
    https = Net::HTTP.new(url.host, url.port)
    https.use_ssl = true
    
    request = Net::HTTP::Get.new(url)
    
    response = https.request(request)
    puts response.read_body
    

Copy

    import http.client
    
    conn = http.client.HTTPSConnection("api.sportmonks.com")
    payload = ''
    headers = {}
    conn.request("GET", "/v3/my/enrichments?api_token={your_token}", payload, headers)
    res = conn.getresponse()
    data = res.read()
    print(data.decode("utf-8"))

Copy

    <?php
    
    $curl = curl_init();
    
    curl_setopt_array($curl, array(
      CURLOPT_URL => 'https://api.sportmonks.com/v3/my/enrichments?api_token={your_token}',
      CURLOPT_RETURNTRANSFER => true,
      CURLOPT_ENCODING => '',
      CURLOPT_MAXREDIRS => 10,
      CURLOPT_TIMEOUT => 0,
      CURLOPT_FOLLOWLOCATION => true,
      CURLOPT_HTTP_VERSION => CURL_HTTP_VERSION_1_1,
      CURLOPT_CUSTOMREQUEST => 'GET',
    ));
    
    $response = curl_exec($curl);
    
    curl_close($curl);
    echo $respons

Copy

    OkHttpClient client = new OkHttpClient().newBuilder()
      .build();
    Request request = new Request.Builder()
      .url("https://api.sportmonks.com/v3/my/enrichments?api_token={your_token}")
      .method("GET", null)
      .build();
    Response response = client.newCall(request).execute();

Copy

    var unirest = require('unirest');
    var req = unirest('GET', 'https://api.sportmonks.com/v3/my/enrichments?api_token={your_token}')
      .end(function (res) { 
        if (res.error) throw new Error(res.error); 
        console.log(res.raw_body);
      });

Copy

    package main
    
    import (
      "fmt"
      "net/http"
      "io/ioutil"
    )
    
    func main() {
    
      url := "https://api.sportmonks.com/v3/my/enrichments?api_token={your_token}"
      method := "GET"
    
      client := &http.Client {
      }
      req, err := http.NewRequest(method, url, nil)
    
      if err != nil {
        fmt.Println(err)
        return
      }
      res, err := client.Do(req)
      if err != nil {
        fmt.Println(err)
        return
      }
      defer res.Body.Close()
    
      body, err := ioutil.ReadAll(res.Body)
      if err != nil {
        fmt.Println(err)
        return
      }
      fmt.Println(string(body))
    }

# Match centre | Football Widgets | API 3.0

The Match Centre Widget shows various statistics, a match preview, lineups, events, H2H, and more. There is much information about the location and the total result of the two teams facing each other.

You can show the team logos, player images and the theme switch. You can also decide to hide all of these. This way, the theme you choose will be shown on your website. There is a light and a dark theme for the widget.

You can change the colours and fonts. You can also delete the Sportmonks logo and replace it with your logo.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/football-widgets/our-widgets/livescore-widgets/match-centre#functionalities)

Functionalities

The Match Center page displays extensive information about a match. The data shown depends on the coverage of the league of the game. A live scoreboard is always displayed, with both teams, livescore and goal scorers. Other relevant information, such as league info, referee, date and temperature, is also shown on the scoreboard.

![](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3244704705-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWspgZhERqy7nYPTldGhL%252Fuploads%252FNo17nJOnIHp2N5WsNjca%252Ffull_page_events_match_centewidgets.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddb65b45f-bbee-4a62-8175-25bc05646bb9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5df8a260&sv=2)

As you can see above, there are several tabs beneath the scoreboard. Each tab shows different data about a match.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/football-widgets/our-widgets/livescore-widgets/match-centre#match-preview)

Match preview

Here you can view data that is relevant before a match. The following data is displayed:

*   Sidelined players
    
*   H2H Results
    
*   Venue information
    
*   Weather information
    

![](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3244704705-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWspgZhERqy7nYPTldGhL%252Fuploads%252FyNLvrgE9Mo9U5kYbands%252Fmatch_preview_match_centre_widget.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0fd1157b-5edc-4e2d-92cd-9af3211c9fc9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bd66903d&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/football-widgets/our-widgets/livescore-widgets/match-centre#statistics)

**Statistics**

On this tab, you can view team statistics and trends about the match. Each statistic is compared between teams.

![](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3244704705-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWspgZhERqy7nYPTldGhL%252Fuploads%252Ffilm49jWTHKvOl0MqzaD%252Ffixture_stats_match_centre_widget.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D814c6b74-1c5e-4ed0-ac5e-396633a0b65b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=47812439&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/football-widgets/our-widgets/livescore-widgets/match-centre#lineup)

Lineup

The lineups and benches of both teams are visible on the Lineup tab. The lineups are visible in a list and a visual formation field. The coaches and formations of both teams are also displayed.

![](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3244704705-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWspgZhERqy7nYPTldGhL%252Fuploads%252FzUydGdzpslGCsv6Gqkup%252Ffixture_lineups_match_centre_widget.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddb511fd4-3a19-4842-9f5b-de3e7e45d0ad&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=eab82f40&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/football-widgets/our-widgets/livescore-widgets/match-centre#events)

**Events**

All events are displayed in the events tab. Per event, it is clear what event it is about when it happened and which player(s) are related to it.

![](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3244704705-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWspgZhERqy7nYPTldGhL%252Fuploads%252FY0Hw8RPxgBTcSXGCr3SG%252Ffixture_events_match_centre_widget.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8845f954-8c77-4520-ac38-3d5d5531a47b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f821e50c&sv=2)

Besides all match events, commentaries are also shown in Events. Commentaries are pieces of text about an event. Commentaries are displayed on a vertical timeline, and important events (goals and cards) are highlighted.

![](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3244704705-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWspgZhERqy7nYPTldGhL%252Fuploads%252FD8cGcUCWQxaQnCC8EFxr%252Ffixture_commentaries_match_centre_widget.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db2efe399-c3e3-4d90-bc69-b3f8660c90ae&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6dd40b63&sv=2)

**Head2Head**

The last tab shows historical data from matches between the two teams. The following information is displayed:

*   Previous 5 (5 or fewer) direct confrontations and their scores
    
*   Total results between the two teams
    
*   Recent form (5 matches) of both teams
    
*   Statistics of past confrontations
    

![](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3244704705-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWspgZhERqy7nYPTldGhL%252Fuploads%252FPI1Snc2wdM4G6CzJwosx%252Ffixture_h2h_match_centre_widget.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd6fc40ce-15fb-480f-bc26-2ff64429fde4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=293696fe&sv=2)

circle-exclamation

Remember that the widget data displayed depends on the leagues you have at your disposal. Also, not all leagues have full coverage on all resources. Check our [coverage pagearrow-up-right](https://www.sportmonks.com/football-api/coverage/)
 for more information about resources and coverage.

# Latest matches | Football Widgets | API 3.0

A much-requested widget is the Latest Matches Widget. This is precisely what you think it is. This widget shows the latest five matches of the team you selected. What is the form of your favourite team? You can deliver exactly that with this widget. You can even show the events and goal scorers in every five latest matches.

![](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3244704705-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWspgZhERqy7nYPTldGhL%252Fuploads%252F1753jwW8KSqXv4tEHVal%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D770d1f1f-4cea-45ef-bf73-a9df2b018681&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b2214e4f&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/football-widgets/our-widgets/team-widgets/latest-matches#configuration-options)

Configuration options

The [configuration options](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/football-widgets/our-widgets/team-widgets/configurations)
 of the latest widget are the same as those mentioned for the team squad widget.

[hashtag](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/football-widgets/our-widgets/team-widgets/latest-matches#basic-versus-advanced)

.

# Next fixture | Football Widgets | API 3.0

Our Fixture Widget shows a snapshot of your team's next fixture. This is ideal for fans who seek information about the upcoming match. The Widget shows the opponent's time, the match, the date, the round and the competition.

![](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3244704705-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWspgZhERqy7nYPTldGhL%252Fuploads%252FNHTrS607pyMav4itSdwM%252FNext%2520match%2520fixture.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd01ebdac-bcc9-4725-bf60-5134669a51ef&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a3e3bce3&sv=2)

**Basic versus advanced**

When using the advanced option, you will receive the following additions:

1.  Colours customisation
    
2.  Custom brand
    

Colours customisation

You can adapt the table of top scorers to fit it straight into your own corporate identity. Designing tables ensures a professional and consistent look and differentiates your company from your competitors.

Custom brand

Looking at the bottom of the basic Topscorer Widget, you can see the Sportmonks logo. With the advanced option, changing this to your brand logo is possible.

![](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3244704705-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWspgZhERqy7nYPTldGhL%252Fuploads%252FXJYxrtdzZjtCDdjJMkO7%252FDifference%2520basic%2520advanced.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5a041075-3afc-4566-8779-765ae6f297c4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3e0014a4&sv=2)

**Also, is it possible to configure a couple of things to your hand**

*   Choose your competition/team
    
*   Make the team/league logo visible or hidden
    
*   Set on dark mode

# Schedule | Football Widgets | API 3.0

The Schedule Widget shows an overview of your favourite team's matches. With this, you can take a look at all the former matches and all the upcoming matches. You can see the date of the match, the competition, the score and future time.

![](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3244704705-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWspgZhERqy7nYPTldGhL%252Fuploads%252FHn7lR1lGvMXfrhBAitYP%252FTeam%2520schedule%2520Brest.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D41d2bf5b-0cef-415e-90f2-cf4ff1be113a&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7b4852f6&sv=2)

**Basic versus advanced**

When using the advanced option, you will receive the following additions:

1.  Colours customisation
    
2.  Custom brand logo
    

Colours customisation

You can adapt the schedule totally into your own corporate identity. Designing tables ensures a professional and consistent look and differentiates your company from your competitors.

Custom brand logo

Looking at the bottom of the basic Schedule Widget, you can see the Sportmonks logo. With the advanced option, changing this to your brand logo is possible.

![](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3244704705-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWspgZhERqy7nYPTldGhL%252Fuploads%252FXJYxrtdzZjtCDdjJMkO7%252FDifference%2520basic%2520advanced.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5a041075-3afc-4566-8779-765ae6f297c4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3e0014a4&sv=2)

*   Choose your competition/team
    
*   Make the team/league logo visible or not

# GET My Leagues | Core API 3.0 | API 3.0

Parameters

Query Parameters

Required?

Description

`api_token`

YES

Your unique API token

`include`

NO

Enrich the API with more data by using includes

`select`

NO

Select specific fields on the base entity

`other parameters`

NO

Include depth

You can use a total of `0` nested includes on this endpoint

[hashtag](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/core-api/my-sportmonks/get-my-leagues#include-options)

`none`

**Related Entities:**

Not available

sun-brightdesktopmoon

Copy

    require "uri"
    require "net/http"
    
    url = URI("https://api.sportmonks.com/v3/my/leagues?api_token={your_token}")
    
    https = Net::HTTP.new(url.host, url.port)
    https.use_ssl = true
    
    request = Net::HTTP::Get.new(url)
    
    response = https.request(request)
    puts response.read_body
    

Copy

    import http.client
    
    conn = http.client.HTTPSConnection("api.sportmonks.com")
    payload = ''
    headers = {}
    conn.request("GET", "/v3/my/leagues?api_token={your_token}", payload, headers)
    res = conn.getresponse()
    data = res.read()
    print(data.decode("utf-8"))

Copy

    <?php
    
    $curl = curl_init();
    
    curl_setopt_array($curl, array(
      CURLOPT_URL => 'https://api.sportmonks.com/v3/my/leagues?api_token={your_token}',
      CURLOPT_RETURNTRANSFER => true,
      CURLOPT_ENCODING => '',
      CURLOPT_MAXREDIRS => 10,
      CURLOPT_TIMEOUT => 0,
      CURLOPT_FOLLOWLOCATION => true,
      CURLOPT_HTTP_VERSION => CURL_HTTP_VERSION_1_1,
      CURLOPT_CUSTOMREQUEST => 'GET',
    ));
    
    $response = curl_exec($curl);
    
    curl_close($curl);
    echo $respons

Copy

    OkHttpClient client = new OkHttpClient().newBuilder()
      .build();
    Request request = new Request.Builder()
      .url("https://api.sportmonks.com/v3/my/leagues?api_token={your_token}")
      .method("GET", null)
      .build();
    Response response = client.newCall(request).execute();

Copy

    var unirest = require('unirest');
    var req = unirest('GET', 'https://api.sportmonks.com/v3/my/leagues?api_token={your_token}')
      .end(function (res) { 
        if (res.error) throw new Error(res.error); 
        console.log(res.raw_body);
      });

Copy

    package main
    
    import (
      "fmt"
      "net/http"
      "io/ioutil"
    )
    
    func main() {
    
      url := "https://api.sportmonks.com/v3/my/leagues?api_token={your_token}"
      method := "GET"
    
      client := &http.Client {
      }
      req, err := http.NewRequest(method, url, nil)
    
      if err != nil {
        fmt.Println(err)
        return
      }
      res, err := client.Do(req)
      if err != nil {
        fmt.Println(err)
        return
      }
      defer res.Body.Close()
    
      body, err := ioutil.ReadAll(res.Body)
      if err != nil {
        fmt.Println(err)
        return
      }
      fmt.Println(string(body))
    }

# Query complexity | Motorsport 3.0 (beta) | API 3.0

Our APIs provide a lot of flexibility regarding includes, sorting and filtering. This flexibility makes us unique and one of the reasons thousands of customers trust Sportmonks as their sports data provider.

To be able to keep providing this high flexibility. We introduce a new mechanic to ensure our services do not get overloaded with requests that take too much processing power.

In our previous API, each endpoint had a limited amount of nested includes, to prevent our databases from being overloaded. However, depending on the combination of includes, it was still possible to make a request which would become too big to process appropriately. We have now introduced the so-called 'query complexity' to prevent this from happening.

The 'query complexity' is a mechanic where each include has a specific score, where the user can combine as many includes as he wants as long as the threshold is not exceeded.

This mechanic allows us to monitor our systems better and keep them up and running. You can expect a higher response success rate and build even more trustworthy applications as a customer.

You can find the query complexity score for each include on the docs page of the include.

Last updated 16 days ago

Was this helpful?

Was this helpful?

# Standings | Football Widgets | API 3.0

The Standings widget shows an overview of the current table. With this, you can see the progress of your team and its standings in the current competition. This could be changed per competition the team is competing in.

It shows the following: Points, games played, wins, draws, losses and goal balance.

![](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3244704705-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWspgZhERqy7nYPTldGhL%252Fuploads%252FK4JD7g0NZmVb3TjgHiUr%252FStandings%2520widget.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfdc709db-cddf-43f0-badf-ab9eb203a528&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cecbbb10&sv=2)

*   Choose your competition/team

# How-to create your widget in three steps | Football Widgets | API 3.0

Hey there, and welcome to this handy guide on how to gain access to Sportmonks’ widgets and use them in your web application. Throughout this guide, we'll go over the necessary steps to make use of our widgets, which are:

1.  Requesting your widget subscription
    
2.  Configuring your widget(s)
    
3.  Embedding your widget(s)
    

So, let's dive in and get started!

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/football-widgets/guides/how-to-create-your-widget-in-three-steps#step-1-requesting-widgets)

Step 1: Requesting Widgets

To get started, if you're interested in any of our widgets, you can easily request them by heading to [My.Sportmonksarrow-up-right](https://my.sportmonks.com/dashboard)
. If you haven't created an account yet, you'll need to do so first. Once you're signed up, navigate to the [My Widgetsarrow-up-right](https://my.sportmonks.com/widgets)
 page under Football Widgets in mySportmonks. This page provides an overview of all available widgets; you can manage them from here.

Here, you can easily request the widgets you're interested in.

When selecting widgets, you'll also have the option to choose between the Basic or the Advanced version of each widget. In a nutshell, the advanced widgets come with more data features and offer more customisation options.

Advanced widget users have the option to configure the colours used in the widget and even use their own brand logo at the footer of the widget.

It's worth noting that all widgets are based on the leagues that you have included in your widget product. For instance, the Livescore Widget will only show fixtures from the leagues you've added to your widget product. So, you'll be taken to the league selection page before you can complete your request. This way, you can choose which leagues you want to include and ensure that the widget fits your specific needs.

On the league selection page, you'll be able to search for leagues based on country and/or name and select or deselect the ones you want to include in your widgets. Once you're finished, simply click the Next button to go to the overview page. Here, you'll see an overview of all the selected widgets and leagues, giving you the opportunity to double-check your request before submitting it.

Once you've submitted your request, our sales team will reach out to you within 24 hours with a price proposal. Once you've come to an agreement on the pricing, you can easily subscribe to your new widget product on the [My Widgetsarrow-up-right](https://my.sportmonks.com/widgets)
 page.

circle-info

You don't need an API subscription to request widgets. However, a widget-only subscription doesn't give you access to the Football API.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/football-widgets/guides/how-to-create-your-widget-in-three-steps#step-2-configure-your-widget)

Step 2: Configure your widget

Once you've created your Widget product, you'll need to set your domain in either the [Widgets Settingsarrow-up-right](https://my.sportmonks.com/widgets)
 page or the My Widgets page. It's important to note that the domain you enter here will be the only one from which you'll be authorized to host our widgets.

So, for instance, if you enter `sportmonks-widgets.com` as your domain, the widgets will only be authorized for use on that domain. This ensures that the widgets are used only on authorized domains and prevents unauthorized usage.

Once you've set up your domain, you can visit the Widgets Configurator page. Here, you'll be able to view a live preview of your widgets and configure them to your specific needs. It's worth noting that the customisation options available to you will depend on the type of widget you've selected, as well as whether you have the basic or advanced variant of the widget.

As you configure your widget, you'll be able to see a live preview of each update in real time. This allows you to see how your customisations will look before you embed the widget on your website. Additionally, you can view the live preview in various screen sizes, including mobile, tablet, desktop, and responsive.

When customizing your widgets, you'll have access to a range of options, including the ability to:

*   **Choose a theme:** You can select a default theme for your widget, choosing between light and dark modes.
    
*   **Show or hide theme switch:** You can choose whether to include a theme switch option in your widget, allowing users to toggle between dark and light modes.
    
*   **Choose a font:** You can select the font used in your widgets, helping to ensure that your widget matches the overall style of your website.
    
*   **Customise colours (advanced only):** If you have access to the advanced version of a widget, you can choose the colours used in the widget to match your branding.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/football-widgets/guides/how-to-create-your-widget-in-three-steps#general-settings)

General settings

The Widget Settings page also allows you to save some general configurations that will be applied to all of your widgets:

*   Domain: Here, you can set the domain from which your widgets will be hosted.
    
*   Timezone: You can select your timezone to ensure your widgets display the correct time information.
    
*   Colours (advanced only): If you have the advanced version of a widget, you can set the colours that will be used across all of your widgets from this page.
    
*   Brand (advanced only): additionally, you can set your brand information, such as your logo, to be displayed in the footer of your widgets (advanced version only).
    

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/football-widgets/guides/how-to-create-your-widget-in-three-steps#step-3-embedding-your-widget)

Step 3: Embedding your widget

After configuring your widget to your desired settings, you can obtain the generated embed code by clicking on the "Get embed code" button located on the Configurator page. This will display an overlay containing the code that you can simply copy and paste into your web application.

![](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3244704705-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWspgZhERqy7nYPTldGhL%252Fuploads%252FT8CwbscUWkBb8A9RkZyZ%252Fembed_code.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D46091fb4-6118-4410-b3c7-44ada8768b64&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2294c10b&sv=2)

To properly embed the widget into your web application, you need to copy three code fragments. The first fragment is the link to the widget's CSS, which should be placed in the head section of your web application page. The second fragment is the container that will hold the widget and should be placed in the body section of your page where you want the widget to be displayed. Lastly, the third fragment is the JavaScript code for the widget, which should be placed at the end of the body section of your page, right before the closing `</body>` tag.

triangle-exclamation

Ensure you paste your widget into an application that runs on the domain you have set in the settings.

And that is it! You have successfully added a widget into your web application.

Last updated 2 years ago

Copy

    require "uri"
    require "net/http"
    
    url = URI("https://api.sportmonks.com/v3/my/resources?api_token={your_token}")
    
    https = Net::HTTP.new(url.host, url.port)
    https.use_ssl = true
    
    request = Net::HTTP::Get.new(url)
    
    response = https.request(request)
    puts response.read_body
    

Copy

    import http.client
    
    conn = http.client.HTTPSConnection("api.sportmonks.com")
    payload = ''
    headers = {}
    conn.request("GET", "/v3/my/resources?api_token={your_token}", payload, headers)
    res = conn.getresponse()
    data = res.read()
    print(data.decode("utf-8"))

Copy

    <?php
    
    $curl = curl_init();
    
    curl_setopt_array($curl, array(
      CURLOPT_URL => 'https://api.sportmonks.com/v3/my/resources?api_token={your_token}',
      CURLOPT_RETURNTRANSFER => true,
      CURLOPT_ENCODING => '',
      CURLOPT_MAXREDIRS => 10,
      CURLOPT_TIMEOUT => 0,
      CURLOPT_FOLLOWLOCATION => true,
      CURLOPT_HTTP_VERSION => CURL_HTTP_VERSION_1_1,
      CURLOPT_CUSTOMREQUEST => 'GET',
    ));
    
    $response = curl_exec($curl);
    
    curl_close($curl);
    echo $respons

Copy

    OkHttpClient client = new OkHttpClient().newBuilder()
      .build();
    Request request = new Request.Builder()
      .url("https://api.sportmonks.com/v3/my/resources?api_token={your_token}")
      .method("GET", null)
      .build();
    Response response = client.newCall(request).execute();

Copy

    var unirest = require('unirest');
    var req = unirest('GET', 'https://api.sportmonks.com/v3/my/resources?api_token={your_token}')
      .end(function (res) { 
        if (res.error) throw new Error(res.error); 
        console.log(res.raw_body);
      });

Copy

    package main
    
    import (
      "fmt"
      "net/http"
      "io/ioutil"
    )
    
    func main() {
    
      url := "https://api.sportmonks.com/v3/my/resources?api_token={your_token}"
      method := "GET"
    
      client := &http.Client {
      }
      req, err := http.NewRequest(method, url, nil)
    
      if err != nil {
        fmt.Println(err)
        return
      }
      res, err := client.Do(req)
      if err != nil {
        fmt.Println(err)
        return
      }
      defer res.Body.Close()
    
      body, err := ioutil.ReadAll(res.Body)
      if err != nil {
        fmt.Println(err)
        return
      }
      fmt.Println(string(body))
    }

# Getting Started | Motorsport 3.0 (beta) | API 3.0

We'll briefly inform you about the features of our API, and then you can explore our documentation for yourself. You will also find out how to create **your** dream application. Sportmonks offers standard REST APIs. Requests are sent with URLs and responses will be returned in **JSON format**. Every authentication is spearheaded by an API token.

Short introduction to Sportmonks:

Now you know who we are, what we do, what we offer, and how we can help you: We suppose you want to get started right away. Head over to our [Authentication section](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/welcome/authentication)
, where you'll create your own API token and create your first request

What else do we cover in the documentation?

*   [Endpoint overview](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/endpoints)
    
*   [Entities explained](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/entities)
    
*   [Tutorials](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/tutorials-and-guides/tutorials)
    
*   [How-to guides](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/tutorials-and-guides/guides)
    
*   [Includes, filters and select options](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/welcome/request-options)
    
*   [Response code definitions](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/welcome/response-codes)
    
*   [A guide on how to migrate from Formula One API v1](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/tutorials-and-guides/guides/migrating-from-formula-one-api-v2-to-motorsport-api-v3)

# Response Codes | Motorsport 3.0 (beta) | API 3.0

Whenever you receive an unexpected response, or are experiencing unexpected behaviour, you should check the request's HTTP response code and reference it with the table below. The following are all possible HTTP response codes for any request made to the API:

Code

Description

**200: OK**

Request succeeded

**400: Bad Request**

It seems that some part of the request is malformed. The exact reason is returned in the response.

**401: Unauthorized**

The request is not authenticated.

**403: Forbidden**

Not authorized. Indicates you're attempting to access a feed that is not accessible from your plan.

**429: Too Many Requests**

Too many requests. In order to make the API as responsive as possible, you have an hourly request limit. The limit for your current subscription can be found in any successful response. Check the "meta" section to find out your limit.

**500: Internal Server Error**

An internal error has occurred and has been logged for further inspection. Please email support if you are receiving this error.

# Current round | Football Widgets | API 3.0

The Current Round Widget shows everything about your favourite competitions and your team's current round.

The Current Round Widget has the following information:

*   The date of the match
    
*   The time of the match
    
*   The score of the played matches
    
*   All the teams playing
    
*   Shows the current round
    

It is possible to configure a couple of things to your hand:

*   The competition/team
    
*   Team/league logo
    
*   Highlighted teams (See picture down below)
    
*   Set on dark mode
    

![](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3244704705-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWspgZhERqy7nYPTldGhL%252Fuploads%252FMGmEfXTkCdibgmvaURd0%252FBarcelona%2520current%2520round.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcabdc2c7-91b3-4211-88ed-2ea41d1fc0e7&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f8c6d989&sv=2)

**Basic versus advanced**

When using the advanced option, you will receive the following additions:

1.  Colours customisation
    
2.  Custom brand
    

Colours customisation

You can design the table of top scorers to fit it right into your own corporate identity. Designing tables ensures a professional and consistent look and differentiates your company from your competitors.

Custom brand

Looking at the bottom of the basic Topscorer Widget, you can see the Sportmonks logo. With the advanced option, changing this to your brand logo is possible.

![](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3244704705-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FWspgZhERqy7nYPTldGhL%252Fuploads%252FXJYxrtdzZjtCDdjJMkO7%252FDifference%2520basic%2520advanced.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5a041075-3afc-4566-8779-765ae6f297c4&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3e0014a4&sv=2)

**Also, is it possible to configure a couple of things on your hand**

*   Choose your competition/team
    
*   Make the team/league logo visible or hide it
    
*   Highlight one individual team
    
*   Decide on whether to use the header or not
    
*   Set on dark mode
    

Last updated 2 years ago

Was this helpful?

Was this helpful?

# Welcome | Motorsport 3.0 (beta) | API 3.0

circle-exclamation

**This version of the Motorsport API will be in BETA for the first few weeks. However, there are no plans for major or breaking changes during these weeks.**

**Please contact us at** [**\[email protected\]**envelope](https://docs.sportmonks.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#a2d1d7d2d2cdd0d6e2d1d2cdd0d6cfcdccc9d18cc1cdcf)
 **if you have any feedback.**

We'll briefly inform you about the features of our API and then you can explore our documentation for yourself.

Sportmonks offers standard REST APIs. Requests are sent with URLs and responses will be returned in **JSON format**. Every authentication is spearheaded by an API token.

If you want to get started right away, great! Head over to our [**Getting Started section**](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/welcome/getting-started)
, where you'll create your own API token and create your first request.

Are you currently using the [Formula One API v1](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v2/formula-one-api/)
 and want to migrate now? Check out our [Migration Guide](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/tutorials-and-guides/guides/migrating-from-formula-one-api-v2-to-motorsport-api-v3)
 to get started.

For any technical questions, you can email our support team [\[email protected\]envelope](https://docs.sportmonks.com/cdn-cgi/l/email-protection#d2a1a7a2a2bda0a692a1a2bda0a6bfbdbcb9a1fcb1bdbf)
.

# Authentication | Motorsport 3.0 (beta) | API 3.0

To make our first request, we’ll need to get authenticated first.

We offer two different options for passing your API token. You are free to choose between the authentication methods. You can also use both of them at the same time. Please note that both methods count towards the same rate-limiting.

*   **Authenticate using a query parameter** You can pass your API token by passing 'api\_token' in your request parameters, like so:
    
    https://api3.sportmonks.com/api/v3/motorsport/livescores?api\_token_\=your\_token\_here_
    
*   **Authenticate using a request header** You can also pass your token via an 'Authorization' header, like so:
    

Header

Value

Authorization

_your\_token\_here_

You can obtain and manage your API token in [**Mysportmonks.**arrow-up-right](https://my.sportmonks.com/)
 The API token is only meant for your eyes and, as such, should be stored away safely. Our tokens have no expiration date and will remain valid until you manually delete them yourself.

When making a request, a code response will always be returned. The following are all possible HTTP response codes for any request made to the API:

Code

Description

**200: OK**

Request succeeded

**400: Bad Request**

It seems that some part of the request is malformed. The exact reason is returned in the response.

**401: Unauthorized**

The request is not authenticated.

**403: Forbidden**

Not authorized. Indicates you're attempting to access a feed that is not accessible from your plan.

**429: Too Many Requests**

Too many requests. In order to make the API as responsive as possible, you have an hourly request limit. The limit for your current subscription can be found in any successful response. Check the "meta" section to find out your limit.

**500: Internal Server Error**

An internal error has occurred and has been logged for further inspection. Please email support if you are receiving this error.

Refers to the id of the sport

integer

name

Displays the name of the sport

string

code

Displays the code of the sport

string

# Metadata / Season Details Type Reference | Motorsport 3.0 (beta) | API 3.0

###

Include: `metadata`

ID

Name

Developer Name/Code

Value Type

Description

9737

Is Qualification

IS\_QUALIFICATION / is-qualification

boolean

Indicates if the session is 1/3rd of a (Sprint) Qualification session

9734

Sprint Race

SPRINT\_RACE / sprint-race

boolean

Indicates if the session is a Sprint Race and the Sprint Points system is applied

164

Has Standings

HAS\_STANDING / has-standings

boolean

Indicates if the session has points which are calculated in the standings

172

boolean

Indicates if the session has the half points rule applied

9736

# Venues | Motorsport 3.0 (beta) | API 3.0

A venue represents a racing track where motorsport fixtures take place.

Use the venues endpoints to retrieve venue details, search for venues, or list venues for a season.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/endpoints/venues#available-endpoints)

Available endpoints

*   [**GET All Venues**arrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/endpoints/venues/get-all-venues)
    : Returns all venues (racing tracks) available in the Motorsport API.
    
*   [**GET Venues by ID**arrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/endpoints/venues/get-venues-by-id)
    : Returns a venue (racing track) by its ID.
    
*   [**GET Venues by Search**arrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/endpoints/venues/get-venues-by-search)
    : Returns venues (racing tracks) matching a provided search query.
    
*   [**GET Venues by Season ID**arrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/endpoints/venues/get-venues-by-season-id)
    **:** Returns the venues (racing tracks) for a provided season ID.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/endpoints/venues#include-options)

Include options

You can enrich venue responses using `include`.

[`country`arrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/core-api/entities/core#country)
 ,[`fixtures`arrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/entities/fixture)
, [`city`arrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/core-api/entities/core#city)
, `metadata`

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/endpoints/venues#related-entities)

Related entities

*   [Venuearrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/entities/venue)
    

Last updated 15 days ago

Was this helpful?

Was this helpful?

sun-brightdesktopmoon

# Request options | Motorsport 3.0 (beta) | API 3.0

This chapter will teach you how to filter out data from our API, which is useful when you want to request specific data and can omit the rest for faster response time. You can filter out data for various parameters per endpoint. See our **endpoint overviews** for more detailed information.

[hashtag](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/welcome/request-options#field-selection)

Field selection


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

API 3.0 introduces the possibility to request specific fields on entities. This possibility comes in handy when you only use particular fields in an API response. The advantage of selecting specific fields is that it reduces the response speed in mainly large responses. In addition to reducing response time, the response size can also be drastically reduced. Let's take a look together at an example.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/welcome/request-options#id-1.-only-select-a-specific-field)

1\. Only select a specific field

One of our new additions to API 3.0 is a name field on the fixtures. The name field contains a textual representation of the participants playing the fixture. Without selecting a specific field, the API request and response would look like this:

Request

Response

Copy

    https://api.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport/fixtures/19408487?api_token={your_token}

Copy

    {
      "data": {
        "id": 18509783,
        "inplay": 0,
        "sport_id": 1,
        "league_id": 2,
        "season_id": 18346,
        "stage_id": 77453618,
        "group_id": null,
        "aggregate_id": 29195,
        "round_id": null,
        "state_id": 7,
        "venue_id": null,
        "name": "Real Madrid vs Manchester City",
        "home_score": 2,
        "away_score": 1,
        "starting_at": "2022-05-04 19:00:00",
        "result_info": "Real Madrid won after extra-time.",
        "ended_at": "2022-05-04 20:54:26",
        "leg": "2/2",
        "details": null,
        "length": 90,
        "placeholder": false,
        "is_final_result": 0
      },

As you can see, the API response is rather large if you're only interested in the fixture's name. Let's select that API field to reduce the response length and size.

We're using the fixtures endpoint. This means that we can select on all the fields of the fixtures entity. You can do this by adding &select={specific fields on the base [entity](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/entities)
}.

In our example, this would result in the below API request and response:

Request

Response

Copy

    https://api.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport/fixtures/19408487?api_token={your_token}&select=name

Copy

    {
      "data": {
        "name": "Real Madrid vs Manchester City",
        "id": 18509783,
        "sport_id": 1,
        "round_id": null,
        "stage_id": 77453618,
        "group_id": null,
        "aggregate_id": 29195,
        "league_id": 2,
        "season_id": 18346,
        "venue_id": null,
        "state_id": 7
      },

As you can see in the example response above, the 'name' field is only returned for the fixture.

circle-info

Please note that the fields that have relations are also automatically included for technical reasons.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/welcome/request-options#id-2.-select-a-specific-field-on-an-include)

2\. Select a specific field on an include

You can also use field selection based on includes. Imagine you want to access fixture lineup information from Manchester City vs Liverpool. Additional to the lineups, you also wish to receive the display names, player images and country details.

circle-exclamation

Please note that we only copied the first player in the lineup in the below examples. Download our full code examples to see the complete differences.

Without selecting specific fields, you will receive a lot of information you don't need. The API request and partial API response would look like this:

Request

Response

**Download full-example**

file-download

66KB

[old\_request\_selecting\_fields\_on\_includes.json](https://content.gitbook.com/content/FnlmCoPQl0hTWxA9V938/blobs/ikJwp54nFAhh0Hz1VGgt/old_request_selecting_fields_on_includes.json)

downloadDownload[arrow-up-right-from-squareOpen](https://content.gitbook.com/content/FnlmCoPQl0hTWxA9V938/blobs/ikJwp54nFAhh0Hz1VGgt/old_request_selecting_fields_on_includes.json)

The API response without selecting on fields

Now, let's select specific fields on the base entities used.

Since we're using the lineups.player include, the first base entity is players. We can select on all the fields of that entity. In our example, you need to select `display_name` and `image_path.`

The second base entity is countries. Just like on the player entity, we can select on all the fields of the [countries](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/core-api/)
 entity. In our example, you need to select `name` and `image_path.`

The new API request and partial API response would look like this:

Request

Response

**Download full-example**

file-download

37KB

[new\_request\_selecting\_field\_on\_includes.json](https://content.gitbook.com/content/FnlmCoPQl0hTWxA9V938/blobs/LmBBg6fyO4uH0yzsftZj/new_request_selecting_field_on_includes.json)

downloadDownload[arrow-up-right-from-squareOpen](https://content.gitbook.com/content/FnlmCoPQl0hTWxA9V938/blobs/LmBBg6fyO4uH0yzsftZj/new_request_selecting_field_on_includes.json)

The API response with selecting on fields

As you can see in the example response, the size and length are reduced significantly.

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/welcome/request-options#syntax)

**Syntax**

This syntax can be used across all endpoints, the documentation for each endpoint describes the exceptions regarding exclusions of some fields/relations.

The table below describes the syntax for the usage of the field selection

Syntax

Usage

Example

&select=

Select specific fields on the base entity

&select=name

&include=

Include relations

?include=lineups

;

Mark end of (nested) relation, you can start including of other relations here

?include=lineups;results

:

Mark field selection

?include=lineups:driver\_name;results

Last updated 16 days ago

*   [1\. Only select a specific field](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/welcome/request-options#id-1.-only-select-a-specific-field)
    
*   [2\. Select a specific field on an include](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/welcome/request-options#id-2.-select-a-specific-field-on-an-include)
    
*   [Syntax](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/welcome/request-options#syntax)

# Teams | Motorsport 3.0 (beta) | API 3.0

A **team** represents a constructor or team competing in a motorsport fixture.

Use the teams endpoints to retrieve team details, filter teams by country, search for teams, or list all teams in a season.

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/endpoints/teams#available-endpoints)

Available endpoints

*   [**GET All Teams**arrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/endpoints/teams/get-all-teams)
    : returns all teams available in the Motorsport API.
    
*   [**GET Team by ID**arrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/endpoints/teams/get-team-by-id)
    : returns a single team by its ID.
    
*   [**GET Teams by Country ID**arrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/endpoints/teams/get-teams-by-country-id)
    : returns teams for a provided country ID.
    
*   [**GET Teams by Search**arrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/endpoints/teams/get-teams-by-search)
    : returns teams that match your search query.
    
*   [**GET Teams by Season ID**arrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/endpoints/teams/get-teams-by-season-id)
    : returns teams that are available in a provided season.
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/endpoints/teams#include-options)

Include options

You can enrich team responses using `include`.

[`sport`arrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/core-api/entities/core#sport)
 [`country`arrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/core-api/entities/core#country)
 [`players`arrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/entities/driver)
 [`latest`arrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/entities/fixture)
 [`upcoming`arrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/entities/fixture)
 [`seasons`arrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/entities/season)
 `seasonDetails`

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/endpoints/teams#related-entities)

Related entities

*   [Teamarrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/entities/team)

# Live | Motorsport 3.0 (beta) | API 3.0

You can obtain all the fixtures that are currently live, starting shortly or recently ended via our live endpoints.

Responses of the live endpoint are highly customisable because many includes are available to extend the response. You can find a list of available includes below, listed per endpoint option.

circle-info

The endpoint to retrieve livescores is:

*   [**GET All Livescores**arrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/endpoints/live/get-all-livescores)
    **:** returns the fixtures that are currently live, starting shortly or recently ended.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/endpoints/live#include-options)

Include options

[`sport`arrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/core-api/entities/core#sport)
 [`league`arrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/entities/league)
 [`season`arrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/entities/season)
 [`stage`arrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/entities/stage)
[`state`arrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/entities/state)
 [`venue`arrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/entities/state)
 [`participants`arrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/entities/stint)
 [`results`arrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/entities/fixture)
 [`metadata`arrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/entities/fixture)
 [`lineups`arrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/entities/driver)
 [`latestLaps`arrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/entities/fixture)
 [`pitstops`arrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/entities/pitstop)
 [`latestPitstops`arrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/entities/pitstop)
 [`stints`arrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/entities/stint)

*   [Livearrow-up-right](https://docs.sportmonks.com/v3/motorsport-api/endpoints-and-entities/entities/live)
